To the program.

Theses on science.

Adopted at the meeting of the President
podium of the Central Committee of the All-Russian Prolet-
cult May 25, 1923 Moscow.

1. Based on the position of Karl Marx, that in various “ways of
production" correspond to historically different "ways of representing
niya“, scientific socialism denies in class society the non-class
the nature of science, both in general and in any of its individual areas.

2. The class character of bourgeois science is determined by anarchism
ical structure of the capitalist system and is expressed not only and not
so much in its direct service to the interests of the dominant
classes and depending on these interests, how many are in the method, point
point of view (method of presentation) and target setting of individual sciences, with
on the one hand, and fragmentation, narrow workshop specialization, on the other.
Its task in bourgeois society is to preserve and strengthen this system.

3. The task of scientific socialism in science is the goal setting of science
towards socialism, the subordination of all its areas to the practice of socialist
construction, elimination of narrow shop specialization, application
The dialectical-materialist Marxist method in all areas
aspects of science, generalization on this basis of scientific methods, critical
the development in this way of the bourgeois scientific heritage.

4. By participating in solving positive creative problems, you
flowing from the above, Proletkult sets as its task
combat active participation in the unfolding struggle on the scientific
front against the resurgent trends of the past - metaphysics
In its various manifestations: religiosity, mysticism and idealism.

Theses on art.

Adopted at the meeting of the President
podium of the Central Committee of the All-Russian Prolet-
cult May 25, 1923.—Mosquaw

1. In a class society, art is one of
powerful instruments of the classist rule of the bourgeoisie. For the proletariat it

U

is an instrument of his class struggle and obeys his instructions

chams and methods of the general system of building proletarian culture.
2. The art of bourgeois-capitalist society is characterized by
is characterized by the following characteristics:

a. Artistic creativity in the whole general trend of fe-
is quietized as “free inspiration”, uncontrolled and
not scientific, and is considered self-sufficient (art
for art), being a narrow-caste monopoly.
b. At the same time, artistic creativity in the bourgeois
society is decorative, additional, in contrast
homage to the wealth-creating productive
labor. It passively reflects nature, frozen or decayed
social forms without creative aspirations for construction
to new forms of social life.

V. Technique of art as an individualistic technique
craftsmanship (handicrafts, craftsmanship), always not only

‚ lagged behind, but was also opposed to the machine technology of the general

natural production.

d. Products of art either exist outside of everyday life, or they lead
from everyday life into illusory contemplation (stylization, chamber and stan-
art), or are externally added to everyday life (applied
quality, decoration).

d. Art in general is production for the market,
commodity production of artistic values.

3. Bourgeois art operates in the above forms
relaxes the psyche, teaches contemplative passivity,
instills in the masses skills, habits, tastes, ideology - beneficial
ruling classes.

4. The task of the proletariat in the field of art is to
to consciously make it directly and actively effective
a powerful instrument of socialist construction.

To do this you need:

a. To subordinate artistic creativity to scientifically conscious
techniques and methods. Replace the fetishized principle of “art”
art for art"principle of socio-technical expediency

` imagery, using all the techniques and methods of artistic
creativity to the extent of their social significance. Walk along the line to-
achieving maximum proletarian class influence,
simultaneously rejecting the bourgeois-fetishistic division
arts into “high” and “low”.

6. Raise artistic technique from handicrafts,
handicrafts to the highest forms of technology.

V. Art should be an integral part of everyday life, as
in active visual forms (posters, advertising, propaganda and prop.,
theater, cinema), and in material-organizing forms (psychophysical
cultural culture, organization of mass action, holidays,
processions in demonstrations, material conditions of everyday life, construction
creation of things).

d. Artistic production ultimately in social
listic society should become the production of values for
consciously regulated satisfaction of public needs
of natural artistic production.

EVERYDAY.

Autumn darkness.
City prison.
Red yard.
There is a patrol in the yard.
Third building,
Seventh corridor.
Dark business
In the white light—
Grilles, doors, locks.
And on the doors
Written in chalk:
“Bol-she-vi-ki.”
Three cubic fathoms of air.
Twenty-three people—
Twenty-three shadows.
Neither the sky
No bread.
Octomushka for a day—
Jokes?
“Sit here and relax!”
It will be six months on the twentieth...
Oh, freedom, freedom!
Good for the one in the kitchen.

Siberia, 1919.

STEPMOTHER.

Olga's mother died. My father remarried very soon.
Small guys - you can’t live without a woman. Mother was short and fat. Stepmother
tall, thin. Mother used to scratch Olga, inviting her with a soft palm.
has flaxen-white hair and says quietly: “Let’s buy Ole
a ribbon, we’ll braid a braid, Olya will go out for a walk and start singing
sing: “Ay Lyuli, ay Lyuli.” And Olya stands quietly, doesn’t shake her head.

The stepmother scratches her hair with a comb, the comb pulls, Olga pulls
head, the stepmother shouts: “Stop, otherwise I’ll stop scratching, you’ll
curly“,

Everything has become, everything is different. There was a lot, a lot of bread. Still more flour
paradise lies in the barn, and the mother bakes from fresh flatbread: tastes it,
what's the new musomehow.

There is a cow, and there is enough milk. And the father is cheerful.

Now everything is different. Stepmother at home. On the streets the sun is burning.
The earth is drying up. There is no rain, cracks have appeared. A cow got there...
I had to kill him by nightfall. `Olga won't have any milk.

The rye in the field is not earing, it is burnt. They finish eating the bread, but new
They're reaping. The father is angry and swears. Olga is sitting under a bush,
My little brother took a nap. Looks along the scorched field,
raises his eyes upward, where the sun burns tirelessly; s" ku-
lachki and whispers menacingly: “Ooh, stepmother!”..

EGORNA.

Capital holiday in Ilyinsky. There's a fair here. From all around
From all the villages, people gather here. They sell, they buy. Women's motley
scarves and sundresses, men's shirts flash. But moremost of all
guys here. We can see their heads, white and black, in all shades,
barefoot and shod, like a flock of birds, chirping, rushing to different hundred-
rons for all sorts of new market items. .

But Yegorka was not allowed into the market. Everyone goes, but he stays at home. Vaughn
Sanka the lame is already coming, the last one.

He needs it too, he can’t sit at home, so he’d let him in
stone.
The sun is high. The village is quiet. Egorka is sitting on the rubble.

There Marfusha chooses a scarf for herself, yellow with large beautiful
flowers.
No. 8 FORGE EXPERIMENTS. ‹ 21

It’s as if someone is pinching Egorka’s heart. Boring, boring. And on
at the fair, the harmonica is playing, the carousel is spinning, people, people...

What to do for fun? Egorka begins to throw fireballs into the pile
chickens hanging around on the street nearby. The chickens take off and cluck. Gets
with a stone at the dog, it runs away squealing, limping alone
leg. “Serves you right, don’t wander around when it’s a fair.”

Egorka goes into the forest. Quiet in the forest. Somewhere a bird was whistling lonely
tit. Egorka lies down on the grass. He is picking at an anthill with a stick.
Ants rush to save their property. “Look, look, look!”
We were eating at no other place than at the fair.”

My heart ached.

The day drags on slowly and for a long time. The fair is in full swing. In taverns
they don’t have time to serve tea.

Egorka, with his hands in his pockets, walks around the village. Near the tavern
stops. - “We came here the other day from Moscow for flour.”
(now many are coming) - they said: “The Bolsheviks closed Sukharevka.
Neither buy now, nor sell.” The sun is setting. They're starting
come, return after the fair. Some have a renewal, some have a direct
Nick, everyone has stories and tales. The boys say; how noble
musicians played at the tavern, as many as four and one such violin
enormous; Yes, how they spun on wooden horses, and how
The Caucasian showed tricks, and how... And Yegorka would have heard. Malice
suffocates, but holds in place. Suddenly he jumps up: “Now, sing-
Those sons of bitches, when I grow up, I’ll become a Bolshevik, I’ll close all the fairs.”

VOLODYA.

Night. Herd of horses. The moon is in decline. It's getting light. Descending to
Volodya River, washing away, ondrank fresh water and when he returned
home, then suddenly I saw that the earth had become somehow different. Sun
just, just rising, illuminating the tops of the trees. Trees
stood silently, solemnly and as if quietly listening to
that is, what the sun-chairman told. It's like a big co-
branre, which Volodya once saw in Yadrino, where his father took him.
There are people like trees in the forest, but it’s quiet like an empty hut. Wonderful.
What he says - n6 understand, but it’s good to be warm. When I finished, everyone clapped.

CHAIRMAN.

Prokofy is a distinguished worker. No one can outrun him
throughout the village on a piebald mare, it would not be possible to drive the herd from the field with such
geek that the dust won’t settle down along the way..

Even if you can barely see him from the ground, he has both a scythe and a sickle, what a mu-
bearded man. And he is a master at working with a pen. Letter to soldier Marfusha
I wrote to my husband, I didn’t have time to punish: how there were bows from my wife and
from his son, from his daughter-in-law and from his brother, things were still going on, and only then Prokofy
everything reminds me: "I wrote, but what else? Maybe the cow calved,
ali“...

Will they go swimming? - Prokofy is the first to cross to the other side -
swims, scares away the geese, puts the pig to flight and shouts: “Boys!”
he drove Kolchak away!“ Prokop took out the red evevda, iritsitsil to
cap, flaunts.

We came from the city to collect the tax in kind. He's right there. Spinning,
intervenes in the conversation: “The Ignatievs’ son is a Red Army soldier, they don’t give a damn.”
it is necessary, comrades. Khundyarov is our fist.” The comrades are smiling

rishi: “Otherwise he will be the chairman of the Executive Committee.”
Prokofy is having fun, he runs, plays, and hears everything “chairman”

“will be” and the heart jumps, and the lips themselves part into a smile.
Hey, you're the chairman!

UKRAINE.

Antipych's brother-in-law arrived. He was missing for four years. When-
was carrying rye, a bag of apples. He tells everything, he tells it. Old people
they gasp, the women gasp, and the kids... hold their breath, just their little eyes
They shine and their jaws move. “Rye is taller than human height;how
fell into a field and drowned himself; you can't see the horse. And it's thick
mother rye, and I will thresh it in it,” one word: Ukraine. Geese,
piglets! And everyone has a garden there - and in it there are countless apple trees, and cherry trees,
There will be tea as big as a fist. Know, live. There is no need to die. And white bread
Always eat the dumplings, don’t mind.”

FROM THE LIFE OF A POET.1.

With coal and in the flood
I scribbled the first verse.
Quiet handwriting, timid handwriting—
Like a straw, a brittle verse,
My crazy childhood—
Sweet village silence.
I scribbled rhymes, humming—
Humming, he scribbled rhymes.
Pack by pack:

Walls, ceilings, jambs

I stained my child's heart.
Of course, they took it for nothing—
It hit me; as it should.

I'm crying on the stove.

And everyone is having lunch.

And I hear my mother complain:

Mom.

Father, the boy has gone crazy—

Playing around... |

I washed it with a washcloth...

I scraped it with a mower...

Whitewashed with clay...

And Lenkka—messed up!—

He ruined my entire hut...
Oh, I gave birth to a phony grief!..

A MOMENT OF INVENTION AND MASS.
MAYEVKA and ANTIKERZON.

Even on the eve of May Day, evenings were held in Moscow clubs—
and memories, and literary and musical - “with all sorts of things”,
starting from the tragic howls of artists with “experiences” and
ending with the tightly padded verses of the left. The districts were buzzing with preparations.
march to Mayevka. The districts were left to their own devices, they refused
services of “central” art workers and tried their own strengths.
This was the most valuable thing. The periphery of Moscow was moving, inventing
The bodily cones in the brain were working at full speed. I had to make it up

it was impossible to sit in a puddle in front of the neighbors, decorating houses and squares,
equipping carnival processions.

THEATER WORK EXPERIENCE.
SIMPLICITY IS ENOUGH FOR ANY WISE.

Political buffoonery in five acts, with a prologue and epilogue, according to
Ostrovsky.

Reworking the text—bS. M. Tretyakov.

Directing—S. M. Eisenstein.

Performed by the 1st Workers' Theater of the Moscow Proletkult.

This piece, staged in May 1923 on the stage of the Moscow
Proletkult, created around itself a lively exchange of opinions and
attracted undoubted interest, especially aggravated by the fact that she
is the first attempt to connect the circus and eccentric theater
within the walls of Proletkult. On this basis—060bo passionate polemic:
can this kind of art have any relation to art?
proletarian life?

INTRODUCTORY WORD.

The main lily of the struggle in theatrical reality is
between two fronts: 1) illusory theater and 2) effective
theater Illusory theater builds its impact on the viewer in
series of “feelings” in the personalities portrayed on stage,
vlyaallows the viewer to “empathize” with the actor’s psychological conflicts,
degenerating the spectacle itself into a certain process in itself. Effective
theater, sweeping aside metaphysics and the unnecessaryness of the so-called stage. "guts" and
experiences, demonstrates on stage organized in words and
human action—one and two—uses all possible scenic
cultural provisions, based on a clear awareness of the impact on
viewer that should be rendered. Thus, in an effective
theater there is an obvious accounting (albeit imperfect, technique
it will be improved along with the improvement of all organizations
tion forms), taking into account the auditorium as a perceiving mass,
to be processed in terms of a distinct social task, and
taking into account all expressive media that are used for this purpose
must be carried out by a stage worker in stage traffic
new
#8 INVENTION AND CRAFTMANSHIP

[A

Because of this, an effective Theater, mindful of its social
the importance of the organizer of emotions in terms of class tasks, based on
today's practice (from which only practice can grow
tomorrow), breaks with the stage illusion of “authenticity”, “unfictional
laziness“ of the performance, ends with the aesthetic (separated from practical
ki of today) by the internal interdependence of its parts.
He also breaks with the means of such organization of the illusory world—
historical and everyday makeup, costume, decoration (Meyerhold).

Effective theater attracts the interest of its audience
nicks—and to the very process of combining elements to obtain
desired effect; he is not afraid to let the most powerful impressioners into the theater
to form material objects and methods of our material everyday life
(the same Meyerhold - “The Earth Stands on End”). He does not hide the attack on
the psyche of the viewer, which is done by an actor who does not imitate, does not
“pretending” that he is working, but really working with his own
muscles, among deliberately designed or placed weights
cabbage soup, which either help him develop a system of movements, or
participate ‚how ‚impressed"representative" elements. Hence the departure from decoration
naturalistic and symbolistic and props, the task of which
aggravate the illusion and create “moods”, moving towards constructive
machines and things that the actor effectively handles.

In terms of an effective theater, it is possible to build an agitation theater,
advertising theater, adventure theater (detective), production theater, -
this is a division according to the purpose of presentation; according to the methods of processing mathematics
rial, we have a bio-mechanical theater, a sports theater, and an eccentric one.
The latter is what interests us in this case.

Eccentric theater conceives of stage spectacle as a process
processing the audience by means of stage influence. Installation
performance is the invention and selection of such provisions that you
are called maximum and psychological effect. This kind of polo-
The rides are called attractions. Actors, things, sounds—the essence is nothing
other than the elements from which the attraction is built; director of art
selects attractions and coordinates them with each other, based on tasks
performance.

In order for the attraction not to be perceived in terms of organization
ical experience as an illusory position, and at the same time
kept the viewer's attention riveted to himself, he should be un-
familiar to the viewer, to alarm him, to intrigue him. In order to
so that it is not felt as an event in which the viewer is in agreement
experiences takes part, but only as a material reason
for one or another psychological effect, against the general background of non-
waning interest, the attraction is built using the hyperbole method,

ocus, parody (hence the philistine “eccentric”). Main

WHY WAS OSTROVSKY TAKEN?

According to the director, Ostrovsky in the unfolding of the action
and the intrigue of his plays comes from eccentric premises, and
His principle of attraction is clearly felt in a number of places.
Oh, this eccentric skeleton of his dramaturgy is crushed by literary
new everyday life, in terms of which Ostrovsky still appreciates
only. Clearing away the eccentric skeleton of comedy, lolu-
We are looking forward to the opportunity to historically and effectively link yesterday’s
dramaturgy © today's technology. Breaking away from the fetish of the “great”
name“, making it serve the tasks of today.

EFFECT PRODUCED.

The experience of the “Sage” was a very significant indicator
of how eccentric theater is refracted in the mass psyche.
The main task is riveted attention and increased response
(with interest) on the attractions was achieved, which spoke for the correct
the very nature of the system of such construction. But there was a whole range of details
undeveloped points that need further work
those The text did not sufficiently link the attractions into a single chain of intrigue;
some attractions that have only interaction value
{vapr., persh), so they seemed to fall out of the plot plan. General
the habit of empathy in the theater, of psychological unity
stage character, to go into an illusory-aesthetic break—
prevented spectators from experiencing the attractions as displays of inventive
style, training. The illusory theatrical performance looks like an organ-
logical-continuous phenomenon; here we have a conscious
innovation on discontinuity and greater activity of the viewer, who
must be able to navigate a wide variety of phenomena,
among those leaking.

It also confused associations and confused the psychological
effeat least that the forms of bourgeois divertissement introduced
here in a parody, are not motivated, and are therefore perceived
"seriously." Characters of an antipathetic (as assigned) nature, pro-
showing miracles of dexterity, at the same time not being discredited on stage,
which again gives rise to confusion. I had to face
with opinions that stated that “officers” (a trio of pink

NINO IS THE TRUTH.
MASTER PROMOTION.

One of the most interesting achievements of Soviet culture is “Cinema”
True." The latest in time. origin art—
cinema, precisely due to the peculiarities of its origin,
can and should be most tangibly used by the proletariat
for his tasks. Cinema-newspaper—what could be more utilitarian?

The colossal importance of the newspaper in our revolutionary era
forced press workers to be more inventive,
and now, in addition to improvements in the newspaper itself of the usual type,
new types of newspapers appear: wall, oral, light and, finally,
cinema newspaper.

“Kino-Pravda” is our only cinema newspaper, published by Goskino
Narkomaros and is led by comrade. Dziga Vertov.

The impact of the film-newspaper is of a different order than the impact of |

an ordinary newspaper. The film newspaper depicts the events about which the printed
the newspaper explains. The newspaper sets itself the task of not only informing

mation about the events that took place, but also agitation; in the cinema newspaper this_

agitation is intensifying. Essentially, the propaganda methods are the same
and the same: tendentious (with specially distributed emphasis)
selection of material (what) and biased installation of material (how). But,
after all, there is a big difference: in a printed newspaper we read, for example, about
achievements in electrification, and in the film newspaper in front of you
work is underway to construct new power stations, we
We see before us the cultural construction of our republic. In
in the second case the impression is much stronger. In the newspaper it is often necessary
deal with such information material, to which, in order to attach
propaganda properties need to add comments. In cinema the text should
reduced to a minimum (ideally to zero), yy film material
newspapers must be organically campaigning. This makes it clear
amount of material, but increasedyou can appreciate its impact.
Kino-Pravda doubly confirms the words of Comrade. Lenyacha, said-
22 years ago: “a newspaper is not only a collective propaganda
distist and collective agitator, but also a collective organizer,”—

how art organizes their psyche in the direction of strengthening

on the days of proletarian festivities, our large industry,

rovye, the joy of the revolutionary construction of a new life.

Ever-improving installation of material. Kano-Pravda uses

She decisively rejected all psychologism, “emotions,” relaxation.
fucking effect on the viewer. She is all in fast and precise movement,

film (t. Vertov), `

Showing events of interest to every citizen of the USSR,

The truth” achieves a strong impression. She captivates the viewer

Difficulty in thinking due to the lack of habit of thinking in concepts. "Kino-Pravda" at

event image is available. everyone's perception.

Russian revolutionary cinematography has penetrated into all corners of our

form of organization of the dictatorship of the proletariat—the Soviet form. Bo-
rotieya in the framework of this form for a scientifically organized organization
labor in all areas of Soviet construction, giving the most

speak of the Soviet organization of economy and state, in the expression
dictatorship of the proletariat.

Answer two:

If the first answer is correct (and it is the only correct one), then

but the combination of them in this whole, called culture, Their type of connection,
target installation of the whole—prin:apially different.

meaning, and not separate, although coinciding, elements of two
different cultures. —

sweat and surplus value from workers and employees.

PROLETARIAT AND SCIENCE,

In relation to the question of the proletariat’s assimilation of scientific
values of bourgeois culture, some opponents of class
approach to science due to the metaphysical nature of their “method of pre-.
poisoning,” reveal a complete lack of understanding of the very essence of the issue.
They attribute extreme vandalism to the supporters of the class approach,
the desire to throw overboard the scientific heritage of the bourgeois world,
as completely unfit for use by the working class.

The slogan “socialization of science”, or
“proletarianization of science,” which was put forward by Proletkult as
a general formula indicating to the working class the path along which
Roma must, through collective efforts, complete Marx’s work:
“everything that was created by human thought - to process, to
subject to critical analysis, check on the workers' movement" and
based on the experience of socialist construction, to make it a suitable tool
construction of world socialism, find new methods and “make
those conclusions in the direction of the specified goal, of which limited drill-
people bound by bourgeois frameworks or bound by bourgeois prejudices
they couldn’t do it.”

Without going into assessing whether the terms are successful or not: “socialization”,
“proletarianization”, which, in the end, has no significant meaning
niya, let's focus on the following:

The Vlass-bourgeois character of science is expressed in the fact that it
served and serve in capitalist countries as a tool for organizing
bourgeois society, an instrument of the bourgeoisie’s domination over the class
themselves by labor, a tool for organizing production and production
nal process in its capitalist-antagonistic form.

It is bourgeois in origin, for the facts of experience are organized
into the scientific system during the period of development of capitalism, in connection with the
due to the growth of productive forces, the complication of social relations
sheny, like a superstructure, fasteningwhich contains the entire foundation of the bourgeois
society; bourgeois in point of view, methods of grouping and unification
facts (“method of presentation”), target setting, sub-
selection of factual material and, finally, presentation.

The separation of science from its real basis - social labor
(fetishism of absolute truth, fetishism of the self-sufficient, abstract

45
90 SR 5 No. 8

cognition), its fragmentation and workshop specialization correspond
the existence of an anarchic individualistic economy, without changing
revealing its essence even in the imperialist stage. his
development.

The science of the bourgeois world as a whole was and is ideological
instrument for building bourgeois culture, it is correlated with practical
such as the bourgeois-capitalist system.

Science, as a system, must become a tool for constructing a path
Tara culture, an ideological weapon in the struggle of the working class and
building socialism,

This is the essence of the “talk” about the socialization of science.

If for our opponents all of the above is “intelligence”
Gentek conversations that the proletariat will never understand,” then
the genuine working class truth of our statement, unfortunately,
feels very painful on his back in his practical home
government work and government management work.

The scientific instrument of the bourgeois world turns out to be significantly

degree unsuitable for his socialist practice.

In general, the point of view we defend can be summarized
to the following provisions;

The economic basis and the corresponding system of supertriples,
or the predominant method of production and its corresponding “epo-
personal presentation" - constitute the cultural characteristics of the era
(feudal, bourgeois, proletarian). As a basis; and superstructures,
have a certain system of communication, combination, relationship
their constituent things, people (classes) and ideas, and—this type of connection,
the method of combining these elements constitutes the essence and difference
a characteristic feature of various cultures. Winding superstructure (social
political and ideologicali) grows out of production 01-
relations and is the instrument through which society re-
regulates, directs, coordinates the production process, production
water relations and strengthens the foundation of social existence
in general.

The method of presentation must correspond to the method of production
social consciousness, social consciousness and social existence. Contents of thought
concepts, like the method of presentation, are imposed by the practice of life, its
spontaneous course of development under capitalism,

In bourgeois society, the entire series of superstructures serves the purpose of strengthening
capture of the strength and organization of the ruling classes, support,
strengthening and development of the capitalist mode of production,
reproduction of capitalist attitudes - therefore, not a single type
superstructures, neither in form nor in content, cannot but bear
class character and not be subordinate to the goals and objectives of the bourgeoisie

0 CLASS APPROACH
ON THE PROBLEM OF SCIENTIFIC ORGANIZATION OF LABOR.

Is a class approach to the problem of scientific organization possible?
labor rations? If possible, what does it involve?

Under capitalism we have such an organization of labor in which
swarm the interests of the producer-worker himself are not taken into account
are. The capitalist entrepreneur is interested exclusively
in the greatest use of labor; the worker himself considers
appears as its carrier.

In this case, the bourgeois scientific organization of labor can
be reduced to the highest possible use of labor, i.e.
to extract the greatest amount of surplus value from the worker
bridges,

The diametrically opposite principle is also possible: approach
to NOT “from the inside”, based on the interests of the producers themselves,
consider the problem from the point of view of labor and therefore consider it
scientific organization, for which the decisive criterion was
would first have the most careful attitude towards workerssilt and then
the tasks would be to preserve it, further grow it, improve
qualifications, etc. In other words, it would be regulated not only
expenditure of labor, but also its restoration and development, care
about work would merge with concern for the employee.

The two indicated approaches receive their results to a high degree
characteristic reflection in the very division of the problem into scientific
organization, on the one hand, of “labor”, on the other, “production”.

This division indicates a certain coexistence
the existence of two apparently different problems suggests two different
series of phenomena that are not necessarily interconnected, especially
subordinate to each other. The phenomenon is quite natural for capital
listic society with its class antagonisms and struggles.

This is a comparison or opposition of the interests of labor
interests of production—remains largely valid for
capitalism and until the end it is irremovable for any sour cream
formations. Only under socialism is this opposition of labor to production

would disappear: both moments will merge into a more general concept, to be
maybe something like a cultural organization,
104 Ca I No. 8

However, at present it seems essential
expand the content of the concept of scientific organization of labor far
beyond the organization of only the labor act. This is an extension
corresponds to the second, later, period of development of the worker
class.

During the first phase the working class is forced to fight more quickly
for the elementary conditions of self-preservation, he approaches work with
aspects of self-defense, which puts forward independent
creative tasks. At the next, later stage, moderately
their real participation in the organization of production and even to
this, when he is just preparing to fulfill his historical
missions, organization of socialist production, - proletariat
forced by the entire course of events to expand the problem of labor organization
to a more general concept—organization of production, if conditionally
accept that labor is included in the concept of productionstva as the main
its constituent element,

Thus, the proletarian point of view on NOT, in contrast
from the bourgeois, on the one hand, it distinguishes the interests of labor itself,
and not the capital that organizes it, as the decisive criterion, on the other hand
goy—considers the scientific organization of labor and production as
a single, holistic task.

Thus, the scope of its activities includes problems not
only psycho-physiology of labor, but also technical, management
chesical, etc.

The next sign by which the two can be distinguished
approach to the problem of NOT, is the field of its application.

The typically bourgeois field of action of NOT is a single
enterprise or group of such enterprises under a single technical
fanatic leadership: this is a natural base for the bourgeois
different NOTES.

Here the work process can be clearly organized:
all factors of production, equipment, quantity
quality of machines, raw materials, labor - a strict correlation is fixed -
the strength of all elements from a quantitative and qualitative point of view,
a pattern has been established in their use in space and
time, strictly weighed, conceived and carried out technological pro-
process as a whole, etc. d.

However, all this fundamentally does not go beyond the individual
new enterprise. “On the problems of organizing labor and production
The thinking and practice of the advanced countries of Europe and
S.-A. United States; however, with few exceptions, even then
later times—mainly the object of her research and possibly
action is a single enterprise or individual elements
No. 8 I E E 105

“It”, Sometimes the object of “analysis can be an entire industrial sector
ity, but even then the formulation of the problem does not fundamentally work
beyond the limits of, albeit a large, but still partial task.

The thought of a practitioner and theorist can also be directed towards
studying the smallest details of the labor process: it can systematize
systematically, steadily, with a kind of inspiration, ever deeper
divide a complex set of labor processes intoforming it
“elements-molecules”, decomposing the latter further into “productive
“real atoms”, fix the analysis on the elements of motion, take into account
shortest periods of time; but, one way or another, considered
from a bourgeois point of view, the scientific organization of labor is essentially
sotvu does not go beyond partial tasks, never rising
to a holistic solution to a holistic problem. .

It would, however, be a great misunderstanding to recognize these
dachas are “bourgeois”, consider them unnecessary, and even more harmful.
Extremely much of the bourgeois NOTE - especially from the sphere
technology—included in the proletarian as its constituent element.

It is advisable to emphasize only the fundamental point of expanding
The basis for NOTES: far beyond the boundaries of a single enterprise.
Where are its boundaries? Where is the field of activity of the proletarian NOT?

In the most general form we can say that it completely coincides
with the field of cooperation of the proletariat. What are its limits?

For the initial period of capitalism it was possible to conditionally
argue that it is mainly limited by the national
national scale; for later periods, especially
swathes of financial capitalism—it has expanded to scale
world By analogy with the fetishism of individual enterprise,
must be considered an illusion, a fetish, the existence of an independent,
self-sufficient production taking place within an isolated
states. This can be sufficiently judged from the significant
imbalance of the modern economy after the rupture of the world
new connections during the war and revolution.

The world economy is now a reality, although the political
physically, due to historical conditions, it may consist of separate
“independent” state entities.

The fact of internationalization of the global production process
is the starting point for fixing the limiting field
application of NOT - if we approach the latter from the point of view of in-

‘the interests of the proletariat, interpreted in detail.

Thus, the task comes down not only to scientific
noy organization of the “technical division of labor” within the enterprise
acceptance, no matter how versatile and deep it may be carried out, but to

and economic problems, issues of scientific organization of processes

ART AND PRODUCTION.

1. ARTISTIC MANUFACTURES OF ROYAL ABSOLUTISM.

The era of manufacturing capitalism created large bourgeois
feudal monarchies headed by nobles. Public
new production has finally become production for the market, and
the remnants of socially organized life gave way to the life of an individual
visually-family.

There was nothing for the artist-craftsman to do here: craft is not
could compete with manufacture, but there was a way into manufacture
closed. The bourgeoisie was not interested, and could not be interested,
artistic inventor; the market is dominated by no consumption
bitelskaya, not a specific value, but an exchange value. Otherwise
while the bourgeois organizers of production cared only about
the personal side of products (maximum savings, processing and
practical suitability). Not only that: manufacturing has so completely supplanted
craft has become such a commanding form of production that
first, the overwhelming majority of market products were supplied by manu-
texture and, therefore, a narrow circle of consumption remained behind the craft
beaters; secondly, the craft had to be equal in manufacture, in
reduce qualifications due to the higher cost of crafts
production and, finally, develop such forms of consumer goods
values that would satisfy the market and would first be quoted
from the forms of the new market ruler—manufacture. Beyond these conditions
made it impossible for the artist to make more or less detailed
work neither in manufacture nor in crafts.

In addition, the old customer, the city, was gradually reduced to nothing.
The cities were now headed by government officials, collective
the life of the former community fell apart, there was nothing to organize and artistic
nik, who was essentially once the organizer of everyday life, more
had no direct connection with him, the new king of society was waiting for him
nature: spontaneous, indifferent and impersonal market with its nonmosuiii
template.

in art. In addition to the need, there was also an opportunity, -og-

3. TECHNICAL INTELLIGENCE AND THE ORIGIN OF NEW FORMS.

Beginning at the end of the 19th century, capitalist society entered into
a new historical stage. A gigantic increase in the concentration of capital,
growth and strengthening of world relations, nationalization of transport,
the phenomenon of trusts and the establishment of monopolies of intranational mass
headquarters—all this was a manifestation of a gradual and continuous
electivization of the productive forces of humanity. Simultaneously with
collectivization of production, inevitably had to collectivize
work and life. Huge industrial cities sprang up, concentrating
containing within themselves unprecedented concentrated masses of the proletariat.
The work of the intelligentsia increasingly became collectivized labor.
nom; banks, industrial institutions, government and municipal
industrial establishments, trading enterprises, technical laboratories

bath organisms, like plants. An increasingly large area of everyday life is historically
was removed from the jurisdiction of the individual and became a social-organization

possible. There was an impact, but it was done for the working class

Acute forms of class struggle, which took an open and
of the entire society, a sharply palpable character, desperate poverty and horror
new conditions of physical labor began to increasingly attract

Ligence. Utopian socialism grew and took shape, uniting

to realize the socialist ideal.

Utopian socialism captured the circle of its ideas and artists
cov. The largest of them, undoubtedly, was the Englishman William

Morrie.

Morris was a utopian socialist. He fought for interests
of the working class both politically and theoretically, but most of all it
was occupied by the thought of socialist art. In a number of articles,
in his books, Morris attacked capitalist society,
in which productive work was not a joy, but a torment.
Labor-creativity, this is the main idea of ​​Morris; but do the work
creativity,” he reasoned, “means creating things in such a way
what kind of person would like to have them, i.e. beautiful things - that means
merge work with art. Morris sharply criticized the cliched,
inappropriate, pretentious formsbourgeois life, he spoke about
its disharmony, the need to build expedient beauty,
beauty in life, and not outside of it, But, being a typical bourgeois
an artist, i.e. artist-craftsman, Morrie attributed
all the evils of capitalist relations are machine. Morris called back to
to the guild system, to the Middle Ages, which he imagined as social
paradise. Having begun the practical implementation of their plans,
Morris organized craft and art workshops. Absolutely
It is clear that there was no widespread production in them
perhaps; the craft could not compete with the factory's technology.
I had to move on to the production of rare items, items
luxury, i.e. radically reject the very idea of merging art with
life. Not only that; hating high technology, Morris could hardly
to give it, at least in the field of external forms; instead, he
studied medieval and Renaissance forms, dealt with the surface
decorating things, making carpets, etc. After a while
time his workshops degenerated into a stamped school of applied
goodness.

Morris's entire plan was petty-bourgeois and reactionary-utopian:
the car won and could not help but win.

MUSIC IN THE LIGHT OF ECONOMIC MATERIALISM.
CHAPTER ABOUT RHYTHM.

The most common form of music, the most interesting for people
in its connection with socio-economic factors is rhythm.

Imitating the beginning of the 4th Gospel, Bülow declared: “In the beginning of everything
there was a rhythm." Despite the certain extravagance of his paradox,
It can be said without a doubt that rhythm is the most important
and the most vital of all elements of music. Yes and not only
music. Already some natural phenomena, such as: uniform fall
the sound of water drops, the sound of the sea surf - give us a certain rhythm -
mic drawing. Already Cicero noted that those falling in equal
The measured period of time of water drops gives a certain rhythm.
The Greek theorist Aristides rightly considers the impacts of bullets
sa, as a certain and strict rhythm. This absoluteness of rhythm is associated
called its origin for idealists with a divine beginning.
Plato (Timaeus 16) sees in rhythm a memory of the absolute, when
Artiet creates a number obedient to the law, to which God also obeyed
at the creation of the world.

For us, such statements can, of course, only have an
heological value, but other conclusions of Plato and Aristotle
about the origin and meaning of rhythm are also painful for us.
great interest.

Aristotle (Roeyea, p. 4; RoNisa, US, 5-7 and ProMeta, p. 920)
definitely makes the development of rhythm in music and dance dependent
from the rhythmic movements of certain works.

Based on similar considerations, Plato (Prophasog, p. 326)
insists on introducing rhythm and harmony into the soul of every young man,
what is primarily necessary for the development of oratorical talent and
trading abilities. Indeed, in classical Greece
the connection between the rhythm of work and the rhythm of the music of the theater was clearly recognized
tra, and the Athenian orator of the time of Pericles, without arousing laughter, could
address your listeners, calling them your fellow dancers.
But with the passage of timeOver time, this connection becomes less and less noticeable.
In the Hellenistic era, with the penetration of eastern cults into Greece,
dance and music are increasingly turning to the service of religion.
No. 8 implementation 133

Religion itself sheds its anthropomorphic shell and
is wrapped in mystical layers, and already Lucian in his own
writing about dance is mainly concerned with the old Orphic
Eros, which initially brought order to chaos and then brought it into
moving streams of stars.

But the main considerations of Greek thought about the connection between the rhythm of music and
ki and dance with rhythmic work were still not forgotten, and in vaca-
le 20th century prof. Wallaszek (Rei Shue Taz) and prof. Bucher (Apey
Tsva Reese) came up with theories about the direct origin
music from rhythmic work, which are largely responsible
they look forward to our constructions. |

If we observe in parallel the action of acute-rhythmic
music on a savage and a cultured person, we note that the first
will react to it with external manifestations much more intensely,
than the second one.

This fact is explained by two reasons: the first is that
the savage is not constrained by clothing, which impedes a number of movements in the cultured
tour person; the second is that the physiological effect of rhythm,
so to speak, inversely proportional to the degree of mental development
person.

The last analogy is especially important and explains
us why the music of primitive peoples is expressed in strictly rhythmic
mic constructions, and melody and harmony have almost no
no meaning, whereas cultural peoples have strictly metric
forms, such as marches and dances in general, belong to the lower class
art and are replaced in creativity by the form of sonata, etc. p.

As for primitive peoples, they are extremely susceptible
are influenced by rhythmic music, and already in the 15th century African
The Chinese traveler Mainers notes that among African blacks
walking, dancing, games, singing, work are performed in metric sizes
measures, and that the most undeveloped blacks grasp the rhythm better than ours
soldiers and even manymany specialist musicians.

It is further necessary to point out some conditions’ social
economic order, which will help us understand the origin
meter and rhythm in music and, in particular, work song.

number of moments that determine the origin of the latter,
It is necessary to note the absence among primitive peoples: first, tools
cops and secondly, production techniques.

In order to build a home, make a boat, weapons,
household utensils or even pieces of jewelry to which savages
have such a great tendency, they need to replace the absence
tools near multiple parts of the body, arms and legs.

134 A 4 V. No. 8

The savage does not know technology. He makes up for what he lacks in patience.
and consistency. Stanley states that in some parts of Africa
The reason for polygamy is the extraordinary severity of the work performed.
employed by women

In Guinea, some natives wear small top hats around their necks.
made of stone, which must be polished due to constant friction. For
The end of the process requires the efforts of two generations. It is clear that the only
The essential condition for successful work will be constant and uniform
repeated repetition of the necessary movements.

Driven by instinct and habit to avoid wasting time
and unnecessary expenditure of force, a person working without tools,
will try to make uniform movements as much as possible
at equal intervals.

Gradually the work becomes more and more rhythmic
character, and Combarier gives excerpts from the general report
French colonies for the exhibition of 1900, which positively states
that in Madagascar there are women's movements preparing the ground for
sowing rice, exactly correspond to ballet dancing, and that the movements
a grain sower in Tunisia, scattering grain on arable land, is strictly worn
metric character. The last statement can easily be
This was true when we observed an experienced peasant sowing a field.

Moreover, these movements, regulated by muscle tension and
replacing it with a state of rest, are completely similar to clock
divisionswith its strong and weak times.

The most metric sizes are quite consistent with certain
types of work. Iambic and trocheus are nothing more than the rhythm of the feet striking
when walking on the ground. Spondee is a rhythm of uniform hand strokes. Dactyl
and anapest—rhythms of hammer blows during the work of a mason, when
The fighter makes two preparatory weak blows before a strong blow.
There is information about the last rhythmic beats among French blacksmiths.
even a special definition: “to make the hammer sing.”

The rhythmic beginning of work, which we considered in relation to
approach to individual work becomes even more important
when working as a maesovaya.

Here rhythm is no longer a convenience, but a necessity. Accepted and 00-
the observed rhythmic efforts and pauses are unconditional demands
efforts to achieve a common goal.

But with the overall work, the strength of individual participants, and even the moral
energy are not the same, and the question of their unification is
issue of labor discipline.

The latter is a necessary condition for the success of the entire
work, and the best means of carrying it out is rhythm
ical work song.

It should be further noted that during difficult joint work,
requiring significant voltage, elements of sound parts
songs appear under the following circumstances:

Physiologically it has been established that with strong physical stress
In tension, a person’s thoraco-abdominal barrier is stretched, preventing
breathing rushes out, and the tongue sinks into the larynx. At the same time
there are so-called aspiration exhalations, completely
involuntary, which are accompanied by sounds. These sounds are
fall with the moment of highest voltage and, therefore, ©
the emphasis of the overall rhythmic work. Gradually both moments coincide
fall and give a working song, first. without words, such as
many Finnish songs, and then with words, but at the same time in strong
in rhythmic ulars, words are replaced by an interjection, for example, russian
skoe “Hey, let’s whoop”, which remind us of our aspiration
origin.

At the same time, to indicate a strong moment of rhythmic
work, musical instruments may be used. We know
that the Malays row ‘to the sound of tom-toms, in Sudan and China many

are absolutely inexhaustible, and those who want to familiarize themselves with them in detail

the rhythm of the work for the origin of the work song, but with an adjustment

For a final clarification of the situation, a small
historical excursion.

The first stage in the development of music will be the work song. Shestrictly
is metrical, and its accents, often expressed by interjections, fall
always on strong takt time. At first, a working song without words, but
further stages of development will be, on the one hand, the inclusion
into a song of words and secondly, rhythmic gestures. In the latter case
the music begins to take the form of a game-dance.

Left and gesture introduce new rhythmic elements into the music,
no longer coinciding with the previous strict metricity. Word in a song
requires rhythm that goes beyond the tasks of declamation, and gesture and dance
are subject to laws governing both temporary and temporary
travel relationships.

With the development of the vanish world of economic and social relations
and the establishment of religion by the state, the latter takes for its
cult singing and dancing and combines them in its ceremonies. But antique
ny theorists (Aristoxenus, Aristides) strictly distinguished the rhythm of melos
from rhythmic division, and developed a very subtle doctrine of rhythm
The mic unit of art is “SVgopos rgo03”.

We know that, due to the destruction of previous economic and
social relations, the ancient world was replaced by Christian
quality The latter, declaring the decisive superiority of the soul over the body,
carefully expelled from the area of religious worship everything that had
attitude towards dance.

Thus, medieval Christian music developed
solely influenced by the rhythmic demands put forward
text. Dance with its own rhythmic laws, expelled from
church, passed into the masses and united with folk song.
And if we compare the melodic cantilena of the church, which developed
influenced by the rhythm of the word, with a folk melody that also reflected
rhythm of the gesture, we will notice a significant difference not only in tempo,
but also in the rhythmic structure of the periods that in folk songs
always accompanied by symmetrical cadences, so good
corresponding to the dance. With the collapse of the feudal-medieval system and
exclusive domination of the church, new music sought to
to understand both flows, but having poorly understood their peculiar rhythmic
laws forforged music into the armor of meter-beat, which, despite
many efforts still cannot be removed from her living body.
No. 8 ssstvo 137

From the above brief historical diagram it follows that,
having updated the origin of the metrical foundations of music from the work, we
must connect the further development of musical rhythm with other
social factors, namely, with church tradition and its
rhythm of the sung word and social games, dancing with their
the rhythm of the gesture.

PROLETARIAT AND FASCISM.

From the imperial war of 1914-1918. both the bourgeoisie and
The workers' clave were not the same as they were before the war. th

{the last decade of the 19th and the first decade of the 20th century were
or the heyday of capitalism. True, even then the periods are washed-
The long rise was followed by periods of depression, decline, and stagnation. But
the capitalist pre-war economy could be overcome without much difficulty
overcame these crises, steadily expanding the economy after each
living crisis. Neto—after the war: The war destroyed so many beams
lives, so many material values, so undermined
the very foundations of the capitalist economy, so destroyed
connections between different countries that the restoration of economic
life on the same principles, i.e. within the framework of the capitalist system, -
the bourgeoisie is unable to do so. She feels it herself and
Mu lost her former calm and self-control and, like an enraged
beast, rushes about in search of environments that would help her
drink the bourgeois system and delay the progress of the impending social
revolution.

The lessons of the war and the post-war economy were not in vain for
world proletariat. The World War was, as is well known,
unlike most previous wars, the struggle was not between armies, but between peoples. Not-
it was necessary to involve the popular masses in a war that took such
unheard of sizes and lasting for years. And the bourgeoisie is not thirsty
sought means to draw in workers with promises and outright deception
and peasants in this “last” war. Through the press—ddtens and hundreds
millions of newspaper sheets poured lies on the people every day -
large masses who were called upon to defend law, justice,
culture, freedom, fatherland. The school, the church,
theater, cinema and, perhaps most of all, treacherous leaders
P International and professional movement. The bourgeoisie then
did not skimp on promises. Through the mouth of Lloyd George in England, Millier
wound in France, Bethmann-Hollwega in Germany, the bourgeoisie and its ancestors
governments in all the warring countries never tired of declaring that this
the last war, that it is being waged in the name of good and justice, in
the interests of the peoples themselves; that at the end of this “last” war
workers and peasants will return to their homes not in the same conditions,
149 rub. 2 No. 8

not the stepsons of the homeland, but its beloved sons, for whom the homeland
will do everything to make their life free and happy.
Both workers and peasants succumbed to deception, believed, and fought for
homeland, covering the vast plains of Europe and Asia with their bodies.
But now the war is over. The armies demobilized. Tens of millions
workers and peasants after four years of war and wild trench life
returned to themselves, to a peaceful life. They found this promised house
heaven? The deception had an immediate effect. The bourgeoisie showed its true colors.
Not only in the defeated countries, but also in the victorious countries,
like England, France, Italy, peasants and workers, instead of what was promised
paradise, they found ruined farms, sick from malnutrition and over-
family work and a sharp deterioration in general living conditions. Ra-
disappointment, embitterment, indignation of those who have seen the light and understood the misunderstandings
The deception of the working and peasant masses knew no bounds. This
the former workers of the pre-war period, the heyday, were no longer
capitalism, when the bourgeoisie felt like the boss of the situation,
and the workers, as a result of tireless struggle, received crumbs of the master's
table.

It was during the war that tens of millions of workers and peasants
participating in it, more and more clearly than ever before,
felt withhowl strength and significance in the state and, having returned © to
lei of the battle, presented for payment those bills that the bore-
juisie, and sharply, revolutionaryly raised the question of the implementation of the given
new promises. And the first year and a half that passed after graduation
war—the end of 1918, all of 1919 and the beginning of 1920—it was time
rapid growth of working class organizations, a time when mass
strikes swept across Europe in a wave, a time when all
the bourgeois world was shaking under the blows of the rapidly advancing
world proletariat. October Revolution in Russia, revolution
in Austria, Germany, Hungary, Bavaria - swept over the confused
bourgeois world, and him. the near end of the case is inevitable. But
That’s not what happened: he was saved by the betrayal of the compromise leaders and...
fascism.

What is this fascism? What is its meaning and significance?

This can be answered briefly: fascism is a special organization
nization created by capital within the framework of the legal state for
struggle by all sorts of - and most of all illegal - means against the workers
class, to fight the impending social revolution. In this
feature of fascism: the bourgeoisie, which in words always stands for
order and legality - of course, for the bourgeois price that is beneficial to her
order and legality - protected by all civil and military apparatus -
rath of the state—in our revolutionary era it turned out to be forced
expected to resort to measures and means that violate its own
No. 8 CLASS STRUGGLE. 143

laws. Since it is not always convenient and possible for the state to produce
carry out gang attacks, torture and kill unarmed workers
and peasants, the bourgeoisie had to resort to creating a special
organization that does not have a state character, but is sub-
maintained by the state with everything it needs.

Let's see how things happened in the “classical” country of fa-
Schism, in Italy.

Italy is one of the countries that won the imperialist war.
And yet the war brought nothing but ruin and ruin to the broad masses of Italy.
suffering: rising taxes, a terrible rise in the cost of living,salary
Italy has neither its own coal, nor its own iron, nor
own oil. Artificially created and greatly swollen for
during the war, military industry during the transfer of the country's economy
on peaceful tracks has sharply decreased. Unemployment took everything
large sizes. Not only in the ranks of the proletariat but also among the poor
peasantry and urban small towns, discontent and bitterness reigned
what a shame. The fruits of the “victorious” war were felt.
And as a result, the years following the end of the war were marked
caused by a wave of mass strikes, both in industry and in
agriculture, and the enormous growth of the professional movement
and the socialist party (the Communist Party of Italy formed
was called only in 1921). Not in any Western European country
our October Revolution did not meet with such enthusiasm as
precisely among the broad working masses of Italy. In the summer of 1920 the revolutionary
national upsurge reaches its highest point: striking workers, not
having fought from the capitalists to satisfy their demands, in
a number of cities, such as Turin, Milan and many others. others, began to occupy
factories and factories, thus passing into the hands of the workers,
who set up production on a new basis. Villagers did the same
economic workers with large landowner estates. Bur-
The juisie was scared to death: the state did not protect it well,
was helpless; the army was unreliable; police in the face of shi-
The entire labor movement was demoralized and inactive.
The Italian bourgeoisie saw its end approaching. But she was rescued
reformist leaders who convinced workers to leave the factories they occupied
riki and estates and rely on the promises of the government and capital
sheets, and fascism.

By that time, fascism was still a minor phenomenon. His
the creator was the renegade from socialism Benito Mussolini, who went over
at the beginning of the war in the camp of the ardent. nationalists-patriots, supporters
war. And at first, fascism acted only as a patriotic organization
nization, ‘demanding more for Italyher roles in international
politics and a larger piece when dividing the spoils after the victory. Trying

1920 and 1921 were marked in Italy by an incessant
bloody terror against industrial and agricultural
workers. Having armored cars at our disposal,
cannons and machine guns provided to him by government agencies,
widely supplied with money by landowners and capitalists,—fascism
made his bandit raids: on defenseless villages, towns
and small towns of Italy, torturing and killing the most active
workers and revolutionaries, burning workers' clubs, editorial offices of social
istic newspapers, worker cooperatives, terrorizing the population and conquering
thus losing one rural district after another. Social
The party initially underestimated the significance of fascism, gave it expression
came into power, and then became afraid and, instead of fighting it,

Last October, fascism, as we know, came to power in

V. Pletnev.

WAYS OF PROLETARIAN POETRY.

(Experience in ideological analysis).

This topic may cause proletarian literary
ditch their old objection: “to indicate the path of proletarian literature-
ry"—this is—“forcing a writer to create by decree,” etc. d., it. p.

We believe that now, more than ever, it is necessary
serious and, we emphasize, clear and decisive criticism of modern
proletarian literature, and hence the definition of those paths along which
which she can go. Moreover, these paths, by the logic of revolution, are already
are now beginning to emerge with clarity that gives the right to speak
about them in rather firm tones. We are not thinking of writing “decrees”,
obliging the proletarian writer to create “this way” and “not that way”,
but, if this “decree” follows from the conditions of the development of the revolution, if
she has already said her word here, then let the proletarian writers applaud
rush to the revolution, and not to the critic who evaluates their past and
real paths and draw conclusions about their further direction.

Let's get straight to the topic:

Proletarian literature already has its own, albeit brief, history.
riya. She has gone through a number of distinct stages that are worthy, and this
One of our next tasks is to cover them consistently.

These stages are as follows; first—period before broad legal regulation—
democr. printing; the second is the period of the legal press, Zvezda, Pravda,
"Lucha", the third - the period of the February revolution, and then the October revolution,
with the withdrawal after October to the group opposing October.—
for example, Bibik from fiction writers, from critics Kubikov, etc. - and
the fourth, which is of most interest at the moment, is the period of no-
howl of economic policy.

The first period is characterized by the complete subordination of the proletarian |

poets based on the motives of Nikitin, Nekrasov, Nadson, Koltsov. Redko in
works of that time, motifs of class self-
consciousness of the poet - this is rather the poetry of denunciation capitalized, poetry
curses to him, poetry of awareness of work, his creative energy, than
poetry of struggle, poetry of attack.

The second period, coinciding by 1912 (Lena) with the general
the emergence of the political movement of the proletariat, is characterized by the fact that
the poet-roletarian of that time felt the power that he could

76

‚
153 AND No. 8

really lean on, and in his poetry there are already motifs of growing
strength, awareness of the inevitability of an imminent decisive struggle. Here
poets are already beginning to sharpen their creativity on a class basis, looking for other
forms, begin to look at poetry and their creativity as one
from class combat missions. This is the period of the poet’s awareness of himself as
necessary for the class of weapons, as a member of a unified army—“we”—proceed
of the collective and groping for the solid class foundations of their
creativity. The struggle of the class tempered the poet, forged him as a fighter; in
During this period, the organic growth of proletarian poetry kept pace with
political struggle of the proletariat and generally represents an exceptional
extremely interesting for studying the development of proletarian literature
tours moment.

The third period is the period of revolution.

And the fourth is the new economic policy.

Let us dwell on their consistent development.

Let's take, for example, the work of two poets - F. S. Shkuleva and
E. E. Nechaeva.

“What little poets, how pitiful is proletarian literature,
if...”—so they will say after reading these names. So be it!

(the first poem was published), i.e. has been in operation for 838 years; second-
roy—glassmaker—10 years earlier; first published poems
labeled 1880, works in literature for 43 years. The path is not small. B
at the time when these poets appeared in literature, the Russian tro-

Let's try to approach the question this way.

What is our proletarian writer now?

Is this an individual, a member of the proletarian collective, creatively
working in literature and having to satisfy the requirements
niyam some pre-drawn scheme?

Or is it something else? Rather, I think something else.

The proletarian writer is a class-historical phenomenon and
household. Class-historical because he does not appear from foam
marine, does not fall from the sky, but is born from the depths of its class and grows,
as can be seen from the above, parallel to its development; would-
this is because its cradle is proletarian life in everything
its diversity, with all its positive and negative
sides, the bourgeois conditions of everyday life, with one hundred
rona, and the collective life of the factory, the school of class struggle, with
the other, by being a proletarian on the sidelines or not on the sidelines of practical
national participation in solving combat missions of its class (trade union,
party) and his complete absorption in these tasks, or with the whole
next to the intermediate ones “little”, “slightly”, “slowly”, etc.

This is, first of all, a living person, dependent on those around him.
his conditions of life and everyday life.

But this is the assessment of the proletarian writer and the proletarian
literature and is completely overlooked.

ON THE THEATER FRONT.

It’s unlikely that anyone now has to prove that any artifice
art agitates, all art is class, all art is political

strictly; Everyone has learned this. Art is a social function, in its `

content and form determined by economic-political
conditions. From them. depends. In a class society, art is always
serves. Forced to serve, no matter what fictions of “freedom” are created.
fell.

For naethe formula of the so-called eti-
ical, subjective sociology, which says that history is driven by
a living, critically thinking person who freely sets his own
long-term goals. Of course, history is driven by a living personality. Undoubtedly.
But so that she sets goals for herself completely freely, from her “guts,”—
Let's argue here. This is a priestly fog. A fairy tale about a man, created by
nom in the image and likeness of God. The goals that a person sets for himself
are dictated by the entire totality of the forces surrounding him—the class environment
doi, upbringing, those relationships that develop under the influence
hiring methods for obtaining the environment for life. There's no way he can jump out of them
can't. And the freedom that seems to him is always directed towards the most
profitable (ideal of “happiness”) implementation of what is dictated by these
forces, these relationships. Therefore, freedom in a class society
there is always only a conscious need (Engelse). This is the scheme
which is based on the iron law of economics. In general,
Of course, this pattern is realized in a whole range of complex
ideological superstructures, often losing visible roots, but invariably
precisely from them growing.

From the cradle, a bourgeois child absorbs habits, acquires
captured by the economics of bourgeois prosperity. Proletarian child
shapes his consciousness by the economy of need. Each of them in mass
becomes the son of his class and spends his life in established (“eternal”
") political, economic and everyday forms - defends
interests of his class, be it a merchant of textiles or a
poet strumming the lyre."

That is why the artist-intellectual, ideologist of the bourgeois demo-
Kratichoskaya myeli with her “evobods”, so - sharahvuleya at the beginning of
revolution. He so absorbed this class (bourgeois) mysticism

What did this primary futurism reflect in class (further,
everywhere—it is precisely this stage of futurism that is meant.—9. B.).

“Futurism,” as the head of this movement stated, intends
threaded Marinetti, “watches life from the window of a luxury express,
< soft seat cushions of a space-consuming car,
from the height of an airplane flight." All these cars were common property back then.
only a big capitalist. And the bourgeois, futurist used them,
like an athlete.

Oya does not want to see the process of creating these insanely expensive and
specially manufactured machines for him. Oa doesn't want to look
into the red-hot mouths of factories and factories, illuminating with tongues of flame
the sweaty bodies and exhausted faces of the proletarians. He takes these carsus
ready. He sells and buys them. And, sitting down comfortably, he begins
with incredible speed look around the landscape of flickering life,
begins to perceive it from a new artistic angle, under the sign
new beauty—the beauty of speed.

“Futurism” of that time was based on the poetry of capitalist
moneyed aristocracy, poetry of the ostentatious side of the bourgeois-industrial
slennogo city.

The worker who produced the car may love it dearly and
spiritualize this love in touching forms, as material
bath labor. The coupe athlete who purchased this car is all
goes into the engine and begins to value this engine above the human heart
chetical and, of course, higher than the heart of that proletarian, with whose hands
this motor is done.

The position of the theater in this matter is especially difficult. At that time
like all other types of original futuristic art,
by denying the “human man” (as they define him), they create
his “man-machine” from dead material, paints in painting
clay in sculpture, the written word in literature, the theater has to
have a depot with a living human. body, which still has no influence
turn the engine instead of the heart, no matter how Marinetti wanted it, or
propeller instead of jello; ka.

How to kill a “human man” on stage and replace him
a man with a propeller in his chest?

There is only one way out - to destroy living, physiological, labor
rhythms of the human body to the anti-muscular illusion, i.e. pro-
natural work, and speed them up until the moment of flickering
machine speed. "Fugurist" overtaking at breakneck speed
car, a live horse, manages to grab hold of this running horse
only the moments of that flickering when the approaching front and
the hind legs form a triangle, - and he draws the whole horse as a triangle -
No. 8. CRITICISM. 179

no one She has not four legs, but twenty-four, as it seems in
while she is running, and he draws a horse with 24 legs.

Marinetti formulates this with slogans: “wireless water”
image”, “down with syntax”, “down with punctuation”.

These same slogansrush onto the stage: - down with the syntax of the living
human body, down with the punctuation marks of human speech,

And indeed, remember the Chamber Theater of that time.

The actor is in continuous movement, not in a state of flux.
consistent, technically expedient movement, and in passing
vii. He moves, gallops, jumps aimlessly, for the sake of technical
the self-sufficient principle of movement for movement. Some kind of
a kaleidoscope of vanity, intrusive, annoying, out of any rhythm
technical, labor, worker-physiological movement. ‘

In the same way, the gesture is constructed in such a way as to kill the “human
‚human“, built against anatomy, against natural work
muscles and ligaments, is built for the aesthetic illusion of movement on
bearings, axles, levers. Therefore, the actor of this theater breaks out
gesture against the working functions of the body. The muscle is placed in a flat
the speed of inverted, dislocated work.

Punctuation marks are removed from the phrase. She starts somehow
then like a top so that the end catches up with the beginning, merging into new beauty
speed. And, deprived of a working foundation, the sound is just as intrusive and
flashes helplessly, like a gesture,

And yet, the original futurism was at one time a phenomenon
artistic and progressive. Breaking with artisanal psychologism
peredvizhniki, naturalistic art, it reflected the dynamics
Miku of the rapidly beating pulse of urban life in a bourgeois city
at the time of the imperialist war, on the eve of the ‘revolution’.

But it’s not for nothing that we now come across the term revolutionary futu-
rism: This is the futurism that its furs have already filled with ‘new’
content, dissociating itself from bourgeois futurism. .

threw the white flag of apoliticality and sat on the same bench with the association

Mensheviks, began to rule quickly “in the thunder and storm” of the revolution, in order
not to be ranked “with the thief and the robber.”

2. IN DEFENSE OF ASSENISATION.

I, a literary critic by profession, approaching literature
contour works, sometimes formally, sometimes journalistically, sometimes outline-
structurally-synthetically, depending on need—that's why I started talking
here about the approach is definitely sewerage, that modern growth
Russian literature, nine-tenths foreign to us, provides enough
reasons for that.

That is to say: nine-tenths of it is “with a smell.”

All Russian literature, for absolutely insignificant quantitative
but with the exception, it is now under the sign of awareness of yesterday.
This is its official flag, the protective color of its kind, accepted
washed up by the naive for the most necessary art of the day.

The latter is simply theoretically incorrect, because at best
Why is such art inactive, sluggishly reflective and passive?
art, necessary for the purposes of today's construction, is non-
effectively operates in the field of awareness of today, ‘and further and
of today's construction. Even where the artist-builder theme is
tically historical, i.e. operates in the field of facts of yesterday and
of a long-past day, even there he reveals, in essence, only
our current understanding of these facts. I'm not even talking about
that... science is much more perfect, and therefore necessary,
an apparatus for realizing yesterday.

It is especially wrong to consider it necessary for today’s construction
artistic awareness of yesterday when
The last operation is carried out following the revolutionary upsurge.
The substitution of creative work on “today” (in the name of “tomorrow”) is tiny
wrestling work on “yesterday”—there is not only a change of pace, but also
in its very essence the phenomenon is reactionary, for it is the most demonstrative
one of the types of escapism from reality, with its imperative
tasks of organization and searches for a way out of “essential troubles” -
into the realm of “the enchantment of sweet soaps” and into outright passeism.

The point, however, is not this, not a matter of theoretical incorrectness.

Or rather, not so much in it as in practically biased
the will of nine-tenths of the fiction writers is still not ours,
and therefore in practical results.

If awareness of yesterday logically turns into assessment,
then the assessment made by the artist-enemy (revolutionaryii), or hu-
a debtor from the “former”, even, finally, an “indifferent” artist—
inevitably and logically turns into... a revaluation of yesterday's valuable
ties—in this case: revolutionary values.

RANDOM OR LINE?

(Discussion article).

In the fall of 1923, the Veroseiysky Congress and the Moscow Provincial
The Conference of Trade Unions in its resolutions on cultural construction allocated
workers' club has a central place in the political and educational work
work among the masses and recognized its main task as the fight against the deployment
growing petty-bourgeois ideology.

In the spring of 1923, the K.O. Union of Metalworkers gave in the Hall of Columns
House of Unions, in front of a large number of invited workers,
even evening of club work at the enterprises of the Union. Naturally
that this evening, which was supposed to show how advanced the Union
implemented the resolutions of the Congress, represented a large practical
and theoretical interest for cultural workers.

For the average visitor, everything was very different this evening.
safely, the choir sang, the physical education clubs showed their exercises
tours, drama groups performed; was even included in the program
collective recitation. But to the cultural workers present
it stubbornly seemed that all this was happening at least in the 20th year, when
there is no NEP yet, and when the struggle on the ideological front has not yet begun
I felt such a fierce character. In fact, in the winter of 1922-23.
the offensive of bourgeois ideology proceeded on a broad front, covering
sometimes even raising slogans friendly to the proletariat; moreover,
remnants of the old way of life also increased significantly during this period
expanded NEP. Kabesides, they defended the positions of proletarian culture
tours, workers' clubs for metalheads?

First of all, it should be noted that the demonstration of “club” works
limited exclusively to the field of art. No reports on
scientific and social-educational work of clubs, at least in digital
rah and diagrams, was not given.

Let us therefore turn to art and focus on work
drama clubs, which are usually the center of club life. Dramstu-
diy of the Mytishchensky plant showed quite decent performance -

an episode from the life of a big city, ending with a “call for do-

nogo Maly Theatre.

The choir performed several revolutionary and folk songs and
left the stage without even showing his skill and causing bewilderment
about their independent existence.

and misunderstanding." And, indeed, it seems to us that we have here

part of her, satisfying her artistic and everyday tastes in the club,
and it also does not mean replacing the club with a tavern with “reasonable entertainment”
Chevyi." Cultural workers need to be able to grasp the bare reality
